***kwab.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwab</a> (26609)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Germanic, cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quappe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Quabbe</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwab</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwabben.html>kwabben</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwab.html>kwabje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weak.html>weak</a>, blubbery <a href = vnd.unilang:mass.html>mass</a>, notably:
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:human.html>human</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:animal.html>animal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tissue.html>tissue</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:such.html>such</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> quivering <a href = vnd.unilang:flesh.html>flesh</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brain.html>brain</a> lobe</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aquatic.html>aquatic</a> plants</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoology.html>zoology</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:any.html>Any</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:several.html>several</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eel.html>eel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fishes.html>fishes</a>:
<ol><li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Lota_vulgaris" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Lota vulgaris"><i>Lota <a href = vnd.unilang:vulgaris.html>vulgaris</a></i></a></span> (burbot)</li>
<li><i>Zoarces viviparus</i> (viviparous blenny)</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwasten.html>kwasten</a> (27582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwast.html>kwast</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laak</a> (128089)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lake.html>lake</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:laka.html>laka</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lakō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:drain.html>drain</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ditch.html>ditch</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:stream.html>stream</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pool.html>pool</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leǵ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> leak, <a href = vnd.unilang:drain.html>drain</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laak</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laken.html>laken</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:laak.html>laakje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:pond.html>pond</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:pool.html>pool</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:lake.html>lake</a></li>
<li>watercourse, <a href = vnd.unilang:stream.html>stream</a></li>

<li><a href = vnd.unilang:border.html>border</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:limit.html>limit</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:frontier.html>frontier</a></li>
<li>marshland</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lāke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:blood.html>blood</a> sucking <a href = vnd.unilang:worm.html>worm</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lieke</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:lijken.html>leke</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:root.html>root</a> shared <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lēkijaz</i>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">leerse</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">laerse</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> syncope <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> unattested *<i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lederse</i>, contracted <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> *<i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lederhose</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:leder.html>leder</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hose</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lederhose</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lederhose</i>), <a href = vnd.unilang:where.html>where</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:no.html>no</a> contraction occurred.
